  // changeType: 000 = formType: 064 : REFR
  wbChangeFlags000 := wbInteger('Change Flags', itU32 , wbFlags([
    {00} 'CHANGE_FORM_FLAGS', // Flags
    {01} 'CHANGE_REFR_MOVE', // Moved
    {02} 'CHANGE_REFR_HAVOK_MOVE', // Havok Moved
